***рубль.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:рубль.html>рубль</a> (590)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:рубль.html>рубль</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rublĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, synchronically analysable as <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">руб-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rub-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Literally 'a cut' (of a grivna bullion).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рубль.html>рубль</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rublʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рубль.html>рубля́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рубль.html>рубли́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рубль.html>рубле́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>ruble, rouble (a monetary unit of Russia equal to 100 kopecks)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">рубли́шко</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">rublíško</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***рубрика.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:рубрика.html>ру́брика</a> (14985)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">rubryka</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">rubrica</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рубрика.html>ру́брика</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rúbrika</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рубрика.html>ру́брики</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рубрика.html>ру́брики</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рубрика.html>ру́брик</a></b>)
</p>

<li>column</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ругань.html>ру́гань</a> (8753)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ругань.html>ру́гань</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rúganʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ругань.html>ру́гани</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ругань.html>ру́гани</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ругань.html>ру́ганей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>abuse, swearing <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">insulting speech</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>quarrel, argument</li></ol>

***ругать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ругать.html>руга́ть</a> (3578)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ругать.html>руга́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rugátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обругать.html>обруга́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выругать.html>вы́ругать</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">заруга́ть</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">ругну́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to reprimand, to abuse, to scold, to rail, to curse out, to swear</li>
<li>to criticize severely, to tear to pieces, to lash</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бранить.html>брани́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">branítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">порица́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">poricátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:критиковать.html>критикова́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kritikovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>ру<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:гать.html>га́ть</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.       <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́лы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:выругать.html>вы́ругать</a>, изругать, <a href = vnd.unilang:обругать.html>обруга́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> т. п..
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-руг-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>. <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ругаться.html>руга́ться</a> (3022)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ругать.html>руга́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rugátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>to call (bad) names, to curse, to swear, to use bad language
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выругаться.html>вы́ругаться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">výrugatʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to abuse one another, to swear at each other
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поругаться.html>поруга́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">porugátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ругать.html>руга́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rugátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***руда.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:руда.html>руда́</a> (9407)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*ruda</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:руда.html>руда́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rudá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:руда.html>руды́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:руда.html>ру́ды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:руда.html>ру́д</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">ore</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated<span class="ib-comma">,</span> dialectal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> blood
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:руда.html>рудо́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:изойти.html>изошёл</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:помереть.html>по́мер</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>rudój</b> izošól i pómer</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>bled</b> out and died</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:руина.html>руи́на</a> (11219)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:руина.html>руи́на</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ruína</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:руина.html>руи́ны</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:руина.html>руи́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:руина.html>руи́н</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">in the plural</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> ruin (construction withered by time or calamity)</li>
<li>feeble man weakened by old age or disease</li></ol>

***рука.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>рука́</a> (57)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*rǫka</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Balto-Slavic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Balto-Slavic language">Proto-Balto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-bsl-pro">*ránkāˀ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>рука́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ruká</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>руки́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>ру́ки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>ру́к</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>hand
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>ру́к</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>ру́ки</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">iz <b>ruk</b> v <b>rúki</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">from hand to hand</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:умелый.html>уме́лые</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>ру́ки</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">umélyje <b>rúki</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">skilled worker (singular)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:держать.html>держа́ть</a> кого́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>ру́ку</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">deržátʹ kovó-libo za <b>rúku</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to hold somebody by <b>the hand</b></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:держать.html>держа́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>себя́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>рука́х</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">deržátʹ sebjá v <b>rukáx</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to have control over oneself, to keep oneself in hand, to keep oneself under control</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:брать.html>брать</a> кого́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>ру́ку</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">bratʹ kovó-libo za <b>rúku</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to take somebody by <b>the hand</b></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вести.html>вести́</a> кого́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>ру́ку</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vestí kovó-libo za <b>rúku</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to lead somebody by <b>the hand</b></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:держать.html>держа́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:друг.html>друг</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:друг.html>дру́га</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>ру́ку</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">deržátʹ drug drúga za <b>rúku</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to hold <b>hands</b></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:здороваться.html>здоро́ваться</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>ру́ку</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> ке́м-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">zdoróvatʹsja zá <b>rúku</b> s kém-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to shake <b>hands</b> with somebody, to greet by shaking <b>hands</b> with somebody</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подавать.html>подава́ть</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:подать.html>пода́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>ру́ку</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">podavátʹ/podátʹ <b>rúku</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to offer one's <b>hand</b></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>моя́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>рука́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сжаться.html>сожмётся</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Mojá <b>ruká</b> sožmjótsja.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">My <b>hand</b> will be clenched.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:развязывать.html>развя́зывать</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:развязать.html>развяза́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>ру́ки</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">razvjázyvatʹ/razvjazátʹ <b>rúki</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to untie/free (someone's) <b>hands</b></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>arm</li></ol>

Зализняка). <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сочетание.html>сочета́ниях</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>ти́па</a> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>ру́ку</a></i>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>ру́ку</a></i>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>руки</a></i>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:под.html>по́д</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>руки</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> т. п. <a href = vnd.unilang:ударение.html>ударе́ние</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>мо́жет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:падать.html>па́дать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:предлог.html>предло́г</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>сло́во</a> «<i><a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>рука́</a></i>» <a href = vnd.unilang:при.html>при</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́том</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:превращаться.html>превраща́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> клитику.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:рукав.html>рука́в</a> (1386)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*rǫkavъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рукав.html>рука́в</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rukáv</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рукав.html>рукава́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рукав.html>рукава́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рукав.html>рукаво́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>sleeve</li>
<li>branch <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">of a river</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>hose</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:руководить.html>руководи́ть</a> (3777)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>рука́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ruká</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hand</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:водить.html>води́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vodítʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to lead</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:руководить.html>руководи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rukovodítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">поруководи́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to lead, to guide, to direct, to manage, to run (conduct or direct with authority)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Per Zaliznyak, the verb is intransitive but has a present passive participle.</li>
<li>As an intransitive verb, the object is in the instrumental case.</li></ul>

***рукомойник.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:рукомойник.html>рукомо́йник</a> (19846)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рукомойник.html>рукомо́йник</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rukomójnik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рукомойник.html>рукомо́йника</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рукомойник.html>рукомо́йники</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рукомойник.html>рукомо́йников</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>washstand</li></ol>

<p><b>ру<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ко.html>ко</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>мо́й</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:никнуть.html>ни́к</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:мужской.html>мужско́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 2-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 3a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-рук-</b>; интерфикс: <b>-о-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-мой-</b>; суффикс: <b>-ник</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

***рулевой.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:рулевой.html>рулево́й</a> (28636)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:руль.html>руль</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rulʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ево́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-evój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рулевой.html>рулево́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rulevój</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> steering, rudder
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:рулевой.html>рулево́е</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:колесо.html>колесо́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>rulevóje</b> kolesó</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>steering</b> wheel</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
